FNV ATMOSPHERE ALPHA-COVERAGE COMPOSITION CONTRACT AUDIT

Observed failure to explain:
Strong OMV atmosphere can leave alpha-tested foliage or grass black instead of integrating it into fog.

Questions:
1. Which accumulator groups own TallGrass, SpeedTree leaf, and other alpha-tested/A2C geometry?
2. Are those groups complete when RenderWorldSceneGraph returns to OMV?
3. Does native image-space effect 0x22 resolve MSAA before or after those alpha groups?
4. Which exact color surface preserves alpha-to-coverage results, and when is it safe to sample and compose?
5. Which D3D alpha-test, multisample, sample-mask, and adaptive-tessellation states do foliage shaders set and restore?
6. Is there a resolved world-color boundary before first-person rendering, or must atmosphere preserve per-sample coverage on the MSAA target?
